Header:

Display your name or your portfolio title at the top.

About Me Section:

Provide a short introduction about yourself.

A project title.
A short description of the project.
A link to the project (could be a placeholder link).

Provide a contact form with fields for:
Name
Email
Message

Add a footer with your copyright notice.
08/12/24, 12:32 - Rohit 16 Nov Kalinga: Ye kya hai
08/12/24, 12:32 - Gullu Broo 20 Sept Kalinga: In CSS
08/12/24, 12:32 - Gullu Broo 20 Sept Kalinga: Design a "Card" component that includes the following features:

Card Structure:

The card should have a title, an image, some text content, and a footer.
The footer should include a "Read More" button.
Card Design:

The card should have a shadow effect to make it look elevated.
When the user hovers over the card, it should scale up slightly (e.g., 1.05x of its original size).
The "Read More" button should have a smooth hover transition where it changes background color and text color.
Card Responsiveness:

The card should be responsive, meaning it should adjust its layout when the screen size is smaller (e.g., mobile devices). You can stack the card's content vertically on small screens.
Card Styling:

Add padding inside the card for the content.
Use a background color for the card, but make the image fit the width of the card.
The footer should have a background color distinct from the card‚Äôs background to separate it visually.

08/12/24, 12:32 - Gullu Broo 20 Sept Kalinga: Create a simple "Task List" application with the following features using JavaScript:

HTML:

Create an input field where users can type a new task.

JavaScript:

When the user clicks the "Add Task" button, the task should be added to the list.
Each task should have a "Delete" button to remove it from the list.
When the user clicks the "Delete" button, the respective task should be removed from the list.
Optional: Add functionality to mark a task as "Completed" by clicking on it, which will strike through the text.
